SELECT MIN(t.t_title) AS typical_european_movie FROM company_type AS ct, info_type AS it, movie_companies AS mc, movie_info AS mi, title AS t WHERE ct.ct_kind = 'distributors' AND mc.mc_note LIKE '%(theatrical)%' AND mc.mc_note LIKE '%(France)%' AND mi.mi_info IN ('Sweden', 'Norway', 'Germany', 'Denmark', 'Swedish', 'Denish', 'Norwegian', 'German') AND t.t_production_year > 2005 AND t.t_id = mi.mi_movie_id AND t.t_id = mc.mc_movie_id AND mc.mc_movie_id = mi.mi_movie_id AND ct.ct_id = mc.mc_company_type_id AND it.it_id = mi.mi_info_type_id;	4
SELECT MIN(cn.cn_name) AS movie_company, MIN(mi_idx.mii_info) AS rating, MIN(t.t_title) AS western_violent_movie FROM company_name AS cn, company_type AS ct, info_type AS it1, info_type AS it2, keyword AS k, kind_type AS kt, movie_companies AS mc, movie_info AS mi, movie_info_idx AS mi_idx, movie_keyword AS mk, title AS t WHERE cn.cn_country_code != '[nz]' AND it1.it_info = 'countries' AND it2.it_info = 'rating' AND k.k_keyword IN ('murder', 'murder-in-title', 'blood', 'violence') AND kt.kt_kind IN ('movie', 'episode') AND mc.mc_note NOT LIKE '%(USA)%' AND mc.mc_note LIKE '%(200%)%' AND mi.mi_info IN ('Germany', 'German', 'USA', 'American') AND mi_idx.mii_info < '7._0' AND t.t_production_year > 1960 AND kt.kt_id = t.t_kind_id AND t.t_id = mi.mi_movie_id AND t.t_id = mk.mk_movie_id AND t.t_id = mi_idx.mii_movie_id AND t.t_id = mc.mc_movie_id AND mk.mk_movie_id = mi.mi_movie_id AND mk.mk_movie_id = mi_idx.mii_movie_id AND mk.mk_movie_id = mc.mc_movie_id AND mi.mi_movie_id = mi_idx.mii_movie_id AND mi.mi_movie_id = mc.mc_movie_id AND mc.mc_movie_id = mi_idx.mii_movie_id AND k.k_id = mk.mk_keyword_id AND it1.it_id = mi.mi_info_type_id AND it2.it_id = mi_idx.mii_info_type_id AND ct.ct_id = mc.mc_company_type_id AND cn.cn_id = mc.mc_company_id;	21
SELECT MIN(mi.mi_info) AS movie_budget, MIN(mi_idx.mii_info) AS movie_votes, MIN(n.n_name) AS writer, MIN(t.t_title) AS violent_liongate_movie FROM cast_info AS ci, company_name AS cn, info_type AS it1, info_type AS it2, keyword AS k, movie_companies AS mc, movie_info AS mi, movie_info_idx AS mi_idx, movie_keyword AS mk, name AS n, title AS t WHERE ci.ci_note IN ('(writer)', '(head writer)', '(written by)', '(story)', '(story editor)') AND cn.cn_name LIKE 'Lionsgate%' AND it1.it_info = 'LD close captions-teletext-ld-g' AND it2.it_info = 'LD close captions-teletext-ld-g' AND k.k_keyword IN ('murder', 'violence', 'blood', 'gore', 'death', 'female-nudity', 'hospital') AND mi.mi_info IN ('Horror', 'Thriller') AND n.n_gender = 'm' AND t.t_id = mi.mi_movie_id AND t.t_id = mi_idx.mii_movie_id AND t.t_id = ci.ci_movie_id AND t.t_id = mk.mk_movie_id AND t.t_id = mc.mc_movie_id AND ci.ci_movie_id = mi.mi_movie_id AND ci.ci_movie_id = mi_idx.mii_movie_id AND ci.ci_movie_id = mk.mk_movie_id AND ci.ci_movie_id = mc.mc_movie_id AND mi.mi_movie_id = mi_idx.mii_movie_id AND mi.mi_movie_id = mk.mk_movie_id AND mi.mi_movie_id = mc.mc_movie_id AND mi_idx.mii_movie_id = mk.mk_movie_id AND mi_idx.mii_movie_id = mc.mc_movie_id AND mk.mk_movie_id = mc.mc_movie_id AND n.n_id = ci.ci_person_id AND it1.it_id = mi.mi_info_type_id AND it2.it_id = mi_idx.mii_info_type_id AND k.k_id = mk.mk_keyword_id AND cn.cn_id = mc.mc_company_id;	30
SELECT MIN(an.an_name) AS cool_actor_pseudonym, MIN(t.t_title) AS series_named_after_char FROM aka_name AS an, cast_info AS ci, company_name AS cn, keyword AS k, movie_companies AS mc, movie_keyword AS mk, name AS n, title AS t WHERE cn.cn_country_code ='[jo]' AND k.k_keyword ='12-21-2012' AND t.t_episode_nr >= 50 AND t.t_episode_nr < 100 AND an.an_person_id = n.n_id AND n.n_id = ci.ci_person_id AND ci.ci_movie_id = t.t_id AND t.t_id = mk.mk_movie_id AND mk.mk_keyword_id = k.k_id AND t.t_id = mc.mc_movie_id AND mc.mc_company_id = cn.cn_id AND an.an_person_id = ci.ci_person_id AND ci.ci_movie_id = mc.mc_movie_id AND ci.ci_movie_id = mk.mk_movie_id AND mc.mc_movie_id = mk.mk_movie_id;	15
SELECT MIN(mi.mi_info) AS release_date, MIN(miidx.mii_info) AS rating, MIN(t.t_title) AS german_movie FROM company_name AS cn, company_type AS ct, info_type AS it, info_type AS it2, kind_type AS kt, movie_companies AS mc, movie_info AS mi, movie_info_idx AS miidx, title AS t WHERE cn.cn_country_code ='[sr]' AND ct.ct_kind ='special effects companies' AND it.it_info ='crazy credits' AND it2.it_info ='crazy credits' AND kt.kt_kind ='movie' AND mi.mi_movie_id = t.t_id AND it2.it_id = mi.mi_info_type_id AND kt.kt_id = t.t_kind_id AND mc.mc_movie_id = t.t_id AND cn.cn_id = mc.mc_company_id AND ct.ct_id = mc.mc_company_type_id AND miidx.mii_movie_id = t.t_id AND it.it_id = miidx.mii_info_type_id AND mi.mi_movie_id = miidx.mii_movie_id AND mi.mi_movie_id = mc.mc_movie_id AND miidx.mii_movie_id = mc.mc_movie_id;	12
